    73→function startTimer() {
    74→    clearInterval(timerInterval);
    75→    startTime = Date.now();
    76→    timerEl.hidden = false;
    77→    timerEl.textContent = '00:00';

    80→        const mins = Math.floor(elapsed / 60000);

    85→
    86→function stopTimer() {
    87→    clearInterval(timerInterval);
    88→    timerEl.hidden = true;
    89→}
    90→
    91→/* ===== LIVE TRANSCRIPT AREA ===== */
    92→function showLiveTranscript(text, mode) {
    93→    liveTranscript.hidden = false;
    94→    liveTranscript.classList.toggle('brainstorm-mode', mode === 'brainstorm');
    95→    if (text) {
    96→        liveText.textContent = text;
    97→        liveText.classList.add('has-text');
    98→    } else {
    99→        liveText.textContent = mode === 'quick' ? 'Listening…' : 'Recording…';
   100→        liveText.classList.remove('has-text');
   101→    }
   102→}
   103→
   104→function updateLiveText(text) {
   105→    if (text) {
   106→        liveText.textContent = text;
   107→        liveText.classList.add('has-text');
   108→        if (isBrainstormProcessing) {
   109→            liveTranscript.scrollTop = liveTranscript.scrollHeight;
   110→        }
   111→    } else {
   112→        liveText.textContent = isListening ? 'Listening…' : 'Recording…';
   113→        liveText.classList.remove('has-text');
   114→    }
   115→}
   116→
   117→function hideLiveTranscript() {
   118→    liveTranscript.hidden = true;
   119→    liveText.textContent = 'Listening…';
   120→    liveText.classList.remove('has-text');
   121→}
   122→
   123→/* ===== TRANSCRIPT BAR ===== */
   124→function showTranscriptBar(text, source) {
   125→    transcriptText.textContent = text;
   126→    transcriptBar.dataset.source = source || 'quick';
   127→    transcriptBar.hidden = false;
   128→}
   129→
   130→function hideTranscriptBar() {
   131→    transcriptBar.hidden = true;
   132→    transcriptText.textContent = '';
   133→}
   134→
   135→/* ===== MESSAGE HISTORY ===== */
   136→function addMessage(text, timestamp, status) {
   137→    messagesEmpty.style.display = 'none';
   138→    const el = document.createElement('div');
   139→    el.className = `message ${status}`;
   140→    const timeStr = new Date(timestamp).toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' });
   141→    const statusLabel = { sending: 'Sending…', sent: 'Sent', error: 'Failed', 'no-webhook': 'No webhook' };
   142→    el.innerHTML = `
   143→        <p class="message-text">${escapeHtml(text)}</p>
   144→        <div class="message-meta">
   145→            <span class="message-time">${timeStr}</span>
   146→            <span class="message-status">${statusLabel[status] || status}</span>
   147→        </div>
   148→    `;
   149→    messagesEl.appendChild(el);
   150→    el.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'end' });
   151→    return el;
   152→}
   153→
   154→function updateMessageStatus(el, status) {
   155→    el.className = `message ${status}`;
   156→    const statusEl = el.querySelector('.message-status');
   157→    const labels = { sent: 'Sent', error: 'Failed', 'no-webhook': 'No webhook set' };
   158→    if (statusEl) statusEl.textContent = labels[status] || status;
   159→}
   160→
   161→/* ===== WEBHOOK SEND ===== */
   162→async function sendMessage(text, source) {
   163→    const webhookUrl = localStorage.getItem('webhookUrl') || '';
   164→    const timestamp  = new Date().toISOString();
   165→    const payload    = { text, source, timestamp };
   166→    const msgEl      = addMessage(text, timestamp, 'sending');
   167→
   168→    if (!webhookUrl) {
   169→        updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'no-webhook');
   170→        return;
   171→    }
   172→
   173→    try {
   174→        const res = await fetch(webhookUrl, {
   175→            method:  'POST',
   176→            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   177→            body:    JSON.stringify(payload),
   178→        });
   179→        if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${res.status}`);
   180→        updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'sent');
   181→    } catch (err) {
   182→        console.warn('Webhook error:', err);
   183→        updateMessageStatus(msgEl, 'error');
   184→    }
   185→}
   186→
   187→/* ===== TRANSCRIPT BAR ACTIONS ===== */
   188→sendBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {
   189→    const text   = transcriptText.textContent.trim();
   190→    const source = transcriptBar.dataset.source || 'quick';
   191→    if (!text) return;
   192→    hideTranscriptBar();
   193→    await sendMessage(text, source);
   194→});
   195→
   196→discardBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   197→    hideTranscriptBar();
   198→});
   199→
   200→/* ===== SETTINGS MODAL ===== */
   201→settingsBtn.addEventListener('click', openSettings);
   202→modalClose.addEventListener('click', closeSettings);
   203→modalOverlay.addEventListener('click', (e) => { if (e.target === modalOverlay) closeSettings(); });
   204→document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => { if (e.key === 'Escape') closeSettings(); });
   205→
   206→saveSettings.addEventListener('click', () => {
   207→    const url = webhookInput.value.trim();
   208→    localStorage.setItem('webhookUrl', url);
   209→
   210→    const backendUrl = backendUrlInput.value.trim();
   211→    if (backendUrl) {
   212→        localStorage.setItem('brainwaveBackendUrl', backendUrl);
   213→    } else {
   214→        localStorage.removeItem('brainwaveBackendUrl');
   215→    }
   216→
   217→    const lang     = langSelect.value;
   218→    const prevLang = localStorage.getItem('recognitionLang') || '';
   219→    if (lang !== prevLang) {
   220→        if (lang) {
   221→            localStorage.setItem('recognitionLang', lang);
   222→        } else {
   223→            localStorage.removeItem('recognitionLang');
   224→        }
   225→        // Re-init recognition so new language takes effect immediately
   226→        if (!isListening) initRecognition();
   227→    }
   228→
   229→    closeSettings();
   230→});
   231→
   232→function openSettings() {
   233→    webhookInput.value    = localStorage.getItem('webhookUrl') || '';
   234→    backendUrlInput.value = localStorage.getItem('brainwaveBackendUrl') || '';
   235→    langSelect.value      = localStorage.getItem('recognitionLang') || '';
   236→    modalOverlay.hidden   = false;
   237→    webhookInput.focus();
   238→}
   239→
   240→function closeSettings() {
   241→    modalOverlay.hidden = true;
   242→}
   243→
   244→/* ===================================================
   245→   QUICK MODE — Web Speech API
   246→   No WebSocket. No backend. Browser-only.
   247→   =================================================== */
   248→
   249→const SpeechRecognition = window.SpeechRecognition || window.webkitSpeechRecognition;
   250→
   251→function getRecognitionLang() {
   252→    return localStorage.getItem('recognitionLang') || navigator.language || 'en-US';
   253→}
   254→
   255→function initRecognition() {
   256→    if (!SpeechRecognition) return;
   257→
   258→    recognition = new SpeechRecognition();
   259→    recognition.continuous      = true;
   260→    recognition.interimResults  = true;
   261→    recognition.lang            = getRecognitionLang();
   262→    recognition.maxAlternatives = 1;
   263→
   264→    recognition.onstart = () => {
   265→        isListening      = true;
   266→        quickFinalTranscript = '';
   267→        showLiveTranscript('', 'quick');
   268→        quickBtn.classList.add('recording');
   269→        quickRing.classList.add('recording');
   270→        quickBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'true');
   271→        brainstormBtn.disabled = true;
   272→        replayButton.disabled  = true;
   273→        micHint.textContent = 'Listening… tap Quick to stop';
   274→        micHint.classList.add('active');
   275→        micHint.classList.remove('brainstorm-active', 'processing');
   276→    };
   277→
   278→    recognition.onresult = (event) => {
   279→        let interim = '';
   280→        for (let i = event.resultIndex; i < event.results.length; i++) {
   281→            const result = event.results[i];
   282→            if (result.isFinal) {
   283→                quickFinalTranscript += result[0].transcript + ' ';
   284→            } else {
   285→                interim += result[0].transcript;
   286→            }
   287→        }
   288→        const displayText = (quickFinalTranscript + interim).trim();
   289→        updateLiveText(displayText);
   290→        resetSilenceTimer();
   291→    };
   292→
   293→    recognition.onerror = (event) => {
   294→        if (event.error !== 'no-speech') {
   295→            console.warn('Speech recognition error:', event.error);
   296→        }
   297→        stopQuickMode();
   298→    };
   299→
   300→    recognition.onend = () => {
   301→        // If we didn't stop manually, recognition auto-stopped
   302→        if (isListening) {
   303→            finishQuickRecording();
   304→        }
   305→    };
   306→}
   307→
   308→function resetSilenceTimer() {
   309→    clearTimeout(silenceTimer);
   310→    silenceTimer = setTimeout(() => {
   311→        if (isListening) stopQuickMode();
   312→    }, SILENCE_DELAY);
   313→}
   314→
   315→function startQuickMode() {
   316→    if (isListening || isBrainstormRecording || isBrainstormProcessing || isReplaying) return;
   317→    if (!recognition) {
   318→        alert('Speech recognition is not available in this browser.');
   319→        return;
   320→    }
   321→    hideTranscriptBar();
   322→    try {
   323→        recognition.start();
   324→    } catch (e) {
   325→        console.warn('Could not start recognition:', e);
   326→        initRecognition();
   327→        try { recognition.start(); } catch (_) {}
   328→    }
   329→    resetSilenceTimer();
   330→}
   331→
   332→function stopQuickMode() {
   333→    clearTimeout(silenceTimer);
   334→    // Mark as not listening BEFORE calling recognition.stop() so that
   335→    // recognition.onend doesn't also call finishQuickRecording()
   336→    isListening = false;
   337→    if (recognition) {
   338→        try { recognition.stop(); } catch (_) {}
   339→    }
   340→    finishQuickRecording();
   341→}
   342→
   343→function finishQuickRecording() {
   344→    isListening = false;
   345→    clearTimeout(silenceTimer);
   346→    quickBtn.classList.remove('recording');
   347→    quickRing.classList.remove('recording');
   348→    quickBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'false');
   349→    brainstormBtn.disabled = false;
   350→    micHint.textContent    = '';
   351→    micHint.classList.remove('active');
   352→    hideLiveTranscript();
   353→    updateReplayButtonState();
   354→
   355→    const text = quickFinalTranscript.trim();
   356→    quickFinalTranscript = '';
   357→    if (text) {
   358→        showTranscriptBar(text, 'quick');
   359→    }
   360→}
   361→
   362→quickBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   363→    if (isListening) {
   364→        stopQuickMode();
   365→    } else if (!isBrainstormRecording && !isBrainstormProcessing && !isReplaying) {
   366→        startQuickMode();
   367→    }
   368→});
   369→
   370→/* ===================================================
   371→   BRAINSTORM MODE — WebSocket + PCM16 audio streaming
   372→   =================================================== */
   373→
   374→function getWebSocketUrl() {
   375→    const backendUrl = localStorage.getItem('brainwaveBackendUrl') || '';
   376→    if (backendUrl) {
   377→        try {
   378→            const url    = new URL(backendUrl);
   379→            const wsProto = url.protocol === 'https:' ? 'wss:' : 'ws:';
   380→            return `${wsProto}//${url.host}/api/v1/ws`;
   381→        } catch (_) { /* fall through to default */ }
   382→    }
   383→    const proto = window.location.protocol === 'https:' ? 'wss' : 'ws';
   384→    return `${proto}://${window.location.host}/api/v1/ws`;
   385→}
   386→
   387→function updateConnectionStatus(status) {
   388→    connectionStatus.className = 'ws-dot';
   389→    switch (status) {
   390→        case 'connected':
   391→            connectionStatus.classList.add('connected');
   392→            connectionStatus.title = 'Connected';
   393→            break;
   394→        case 'connecting':
   395→            connectionStatus.classList.add('connecting');
   396→            connectionStatus.title = 'Connecting…';
   397→            break;
   398→        case 'idle':
   399→            connectionStatus.classList.add('idle');
   400→            connectionStatus.title = 'Ready';
   401→            break;
   402→        default:
   403→            connectionStatus.title = 'Disconnected';
   404→    }
   405→}
   406→
   407→function initializeWebSocket() {
   408→    ws = new WebSocket(getWebSocketUrl());
   409→
   410→    ws.onopen = () => {
   411→        wsConnected = true;
   412→        updateConnectionStatus('idle');
   413→        if (autoStart && !isBrainstormRecording && !isAutoStarted) {
   414→            isAutoStarted = true;
   415→            startBrainstormRecording();
   416→        }
   417→    };
   418→
   419→    ws.onerror = (error) => {
   420→        console.error('WebSocket error:', error);
   421→        updateConnectionStatus('disconnected');
   422→    };
   423→
   424→    ws.onmessage = (event) => {
   425→        const data = JSON.parse(event.data);
   426→        switch (data.type) {
   427→            case 'status':
   428→                updateConnectionStatus(data.status);
   429→                if (data.status === 'idle') {
   430→                    stopTimer();
   431→                    if (_awaitingBrainstormResult) {
   432→                        _awaitingBrainstormResult = false;
   433→                        isBrainstormProcessing    = false;
   434→                        quickBtn.disabled         = false;
   435→                        brainstormBtn.disabled    = false;
   436→                        micHint.textContent       = '';
   437→                        micHint.classList.remove('active', 'brainstorm-active', 'processing');
   438→                        hideLiveTranscript();
   439→                        updateReplayButtonState();
   440→                        const finalText = brainstormTranscript.trim();
   441→                        brainstormTranscript = '';
   442→                        if (finalText) {
   443→                            showTranscriptBar(finalText, 'brainstorm');
   444→                        }
   445→                    }
   446→                }
   447→                break;
   448→
   449→            case 'text':
   450→                if (data.isNewResponse) {
   451→                    brainstormTranscript = data.content;
   452→                } else {
   453→                    brainstormTranscript += data.content;
   454→                }
   455→                if (isBrainstormProcessing) {
   456→                    updateLiveText(brainstormTranscript);
   457→                }
   458→                break;
   459→
   460→            case 'error':
   461→                alert(data.content);
   462→                updateConnectionStatus('idle');
   463→                _awaitingBrainstormResult = false;
   464→                isBrainstormProcessing    = false;
   465→                quickBtn.disabled         = false;
   466→                brainstormBtn.disabled    = false;
   467→                micHint.textContent       = '';
   468→                micHint.classList.remove('active', 'brainstorm-active', 'processing');
   469→                hideLiveTranscript();
   470→                brainstormTranscript = '';
   471→                updateReplayButtonState();
   472→                break;
   473→        }
   474→    };
   475→
   476→    ws.onclose = () => {
   477→        wsConnected            = false;
   478→        isBrainstormRecording  = false;
   479→        isStopping             = false;
   480→        updateConnectionStatus('disconnected');
   481→        brainstormBtn.classList.remove('recording');
   482→        brainstormRing.classList.remove('recording');
   483→        brainstormBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'false');
   484→        // Reconnect automatically
   485→        setTimeout(initializeWebSocket, 1000);
   486→    };
   487→}
   488→
   489→/* ===== Audio processing ===== */
   490→function createAudioProcessor() {
   491→    processor = audioContext.createScriptProcessor(4096, 1, 1);
   492→    processor.onaudioprocess = async (e) => {
   493→        if (!isBrainstormRecording && !isStopping) return;
   494→
   495→        const inputData = e.inputBuffer.getChannelData(0);
   496→        const pcmData   = new Int16Array(inputData.length);
   497→        for (let i = 0; i < inputData.length; i++) {
   498→            pcmData[i] = Math.max(-32768, Math.min(32767, Math.floor(inputData[i] * 32767)));
   499→        }
   500→
   501→        const combined = new Int16Array(audioBuffer.length + pcmData.length);
   502→        combined.set(audioBuffer);
   503→        combined.set(pcmData, audioBuffer.length);
   504→        audioBuffer = combined;
   505→
   506→        if (audioBuffer.length >= 24000) {
   507→            const sendBuffer = audioBuffer.slice(0, 24000);
   508→            audioBuffer      = audioBuffer.slice(24000);
   509→
   510→            if (ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
   511→                ws.send(sendBuffer.buffer);
   512→
   513→                if (storageAvailable && currentSessionId && sessionStartTime) {
   514→                    const deltaMs = performance.now() - sessionStartTime;
   515→                    await appendChunk(currentSessionId, {
   516→                        seq: chunkSeq++, deltaMs,
   517→                        kind: 'audio', payload: sendBuffer.buffer, byteLength: sendBuffer.byteLength,
   518→                    });
   519→                }
   520→            }
   521→        }
   522→    };
   523→    return processor;
   524→}
   525→
   526→async function initAudio(audioStream) {
   527→    if (audioContext && audioContext.state !== 'closed') {
   528→        try { await audioContext.close(); } catch (_) {}
   529→    }
   530→    audioContext = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
   531→    source       = audioContext.createMediaStreamSource(audioStream);
   532→    processor    = createAudioProcessor();
   533→    source.connect(processor);
   534→    processor.connect(audioContext.destination);
   535→    if (audioContext.state === 'suspended') await audioContext.resume();
   536→}
   537→
   538→function cleanupAudioResources() {
   539→    if (stream) {
   540→        stream.getTracks().forEach(t => t.stop());
   541→        stream = null;
   542→    }
   543→    if (audioContext && audioContext.state !== 'closed') {
   544→        audioContext.close().catch(() => {});
   545→        audioContext = null;
   546→    }
   547→    source            = null;
   548→    processor         = null;
   549→    streamInitialized = false;
   550→}
   551→
   552→async function startBrainstormRecording() {
   553→    if (isBrainstormRecording || isListening || isBrainstormProcessing || isReplaying) return;
   554→
   555→    if (!ws || ws.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN) {
   556→        alert('WebSocket is not connected. Please wait or check the backend URL in Settings.');
   557→        return;
   558→    }
   559→
   560→    try {
   561→        brainstormTranscript = '';
   562→        hideTranscriptBar();
   563→
   564→        // Re-use existing stream if still alive, else reinit
   565→        let streamActive = false;
   566→        try {
   567→            streamActive = streamInitialized && stream && stream.active &&
   568→                           stream.getTracks().every(t => t.readyState === 'live');
   569→        } catch (_) { streamActive = false; }
   570→
   571→        if (!streamActive) {
   572→            cleanupAudioResources();
   573→            stream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({
   574→                audio: { channelCount: 1, echoCancellation: true, noiseSuppression: true, autoGainControl: true },
   575→            });
   576→            streamInitialized = true;
   577→        }
   578→
   579→        if (!audioContext || audioContext.state === 'closed') {
   580→            await initAudio(stream);
   581→        } else if (audioContext.state === 'suspended') {
   582→            await audioContext.resume();
   583→        }
   584→
   585→        isBrainstormRecording = true;
   586→        if (storageAvailable) await createSession();
   587→
   588→        const selectedModel = modelSelect ? modelSelect.value : 'gpt-realtime-mini-2025-12-15';
   589→        ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: 'start_recording', model: selectedModel }));
   590→
   591→        startTimer();
   592→        brainstormBtn.classList.add('recording');
   593→        brainstormRing.classList.add('recording');
   594→        brainstormBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'true');
   595→        quickBtn.disabled    = true;
   596→        replayButton.disabled = true;
   597→        micHint.textContent  = 'Recording… tap Brainstorm to stop';
   598→        micHint.classList.add('active', 'brainstorm-active');
   599→        micHint.classList.remove('processing');
   600→        showLiveTranscript('', 'brainstorm');
   601→
   602→    } catch (error) {
   603→        console.error('Error starting Brainstorm:', error);
   604→        isBrainstormRecording = false;
   605→        alert('Error accessing microphone: ' + error.message);
   606→    }
   607→}
   608→
   609→async function stopBrainstormRecording() {
   610→    if (!isBrainstormRecording) return;
   611→
   612→    isStopping            = true;
   613→    isBrainstormRecording = false;
   614→    const durationMs      = sessionStartTime ? performance.now() - sessionStartTime : 0;
   615→
   616→    stopTimer();
   617→    brainstormBtn.classList.remove('recording');
   618→    brainstormRing.classList.remove('recording');
   619→    brainstormBtn.setAttribute('aria-pressed', 'false');
   620→    brainstormBtn.disabled = true; // keep disabled until WS idle
   621→
   622→    micHint.textContent = 'Processing…';
   623→    micHint.classList.remove('brainstorm-active');
   624→    micHint.classList.add('processing');
   625→
   626→    // Allow any in-flight onaudioprocess callbacks to complete
   627→    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 100));
   628→
   629→    // Flush remaining audio buffer
   630→    if (audioBuffer.length > 0 && ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
   631→        const sendBuffer = audioBuffer.slice();
   632→        ws.send(sendBuffer.buffer);
   633→        if (storageAvailable && currentSessionId && sessionStartTime) {
   634→            const deltaMs = performance.now() - sessionStartTime;
   635→            await appendChunk(currentSessionId, {
   636→                seq: chunkSeq++, deltaMs,
   637→                kind: 'audio', payload: sendBuffer.buffer, byteLength: sendBuffer.byteLength,
   638→            });
   639→        }
   640→        audioBuffer = new Int16Array(0);
   641→    }
   642→
   643→    isStopping = false;
   644→
   645→    // Small delay to ensure all audio sent before stop signal
   646→    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
   647→    ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: 'stop_recording' }));
   648→
   649→    if (storageAvailable && currentSessionId) {
   650→        await completeSession(currentSessionId, durationMs);
   651→        currentSessionId  = null;
   652→        sessionStartTime  = null;
   653→        chunkSeq          = 0;
   654→    }
   655→
   656→    // Switch to processing state — WS idle handler will finish the flow
   657→    isBrainstormProcessing    = true;
   658→    _awaitingBrainstormResult = true;
   659→    liveText.textContent      = 'Processing…';
   660→    liveText.classList.remove('has-text');
   661→}
   662→
   663→brainstormBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {
   664→    if (isBrainstormRecording) {
   665→        stopBrainstormRecording();
   666→    } else if (!isListening && !isBrainstormProcessing && !isReplaying) {
   667→        startBrainstormRecording();
   668→    }
   669→});
   670→
   671→/* ===================================================
   672→   REPLAY — sends stored IndexedDB audio through WS
   673→   =================================================== */
   674→
   675→async function replayLastRecording() {
   676→    if (isBrainstormRecording || isReplaying || isListening || isBrainstormProcessing) return;
   677→
   678→    const session = await getLatestCompletedSession();
   679→    if (!session) {
   680→        alert('No completed recording found to replay.');
   681→        return;
   682→    }
   683→
   684→    isReplaying              = true;
   685→    quickBtn.disabled        = true;
   686→    brainstormBtn.disabled   = true;
   687→    replayButton.disabled    = true;
   688→    replayButton.classList.add('replaying');
   689→    brainstormTranscript     = '';
   690→
   691→    try {
   692→        hideTranscriptBar();
   693→        const chunks = await getSessionChunks(session.id);
   694→        if (chunks.length === 0) throw new Error('No audio chunks found for session');
   695→
   696→        // Wait for WS if needed
   697→        if (!wsConnected || ws.readyState !== WebSocket.OPEN) {
   698→            await new Promise(resolve => {
   699→                const check = setInterval(() => {
   700→                    if (wsConnected && ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) { clearInterval(check); resolve(); }
   701→                }, 100);
   702→            });
   703→        }
   704→
   705→        const selectedModel = modelSelect ? modelSelect.value : 'gpt-realtime-mini-2025-12-15';
   706→        ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: 'start_recording', model: selectedModel }));
   707→        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 200));
   708→
   709→        for (const chunk of chunks.filter(c => c.kind === 'audio' && c.payload)) {
   710→            if (ws.readyState === WebSocket.OPEN) {
   711→                ws.send(chunk.payload);
   712→            } else {
   713→                throw new Error('WebSocket closed during replay');
   714→            }
   715→        }
   716→
   717→        ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: 'stop_recording' }));
   718→
   719→        isBrainstormProcessing    = true;
   720→        _awaitingBrainstormResult = true;
   721→        micHint.textContent       = 'Processing replay…';
   722→        micHint.classList.add('active', 'processing');
   723→        micHint.classList.remove('brainstorm-active');
   724→        showLiveTranscript('Processing replay…', 'brainstorm');
   725→
   726→    } catch (error) {
   727→        console.error('Replay error:', error);
   728→        alert('Error replaying recording: ' + error.message);
   729→        isBrainstormProcessing    = false;
   730→        _awaitingBrainstormResult = false;
   731→        micHint.textContent       = '';
   732→        micHint.classList.remove('active', 'processing');
   733→        quickBtn.disabled        = false;
   734→        brainstormBtn.disabled   = false;
   735→    } finally {
   736→        isReplaying = false;
   737→        replayButton.classList.remove('replaying');
   738→        updateReplayButtonState();
   739→        // quickBtn/brainstormBtn re-enabled by WS idle handler if processing started
   740→        if (!isBrainstormProcessing) {
   741→            quickBtn.disabled      = false;
   742→            brainstormBtn.disabled = false;
   743→        }
   744→    }
   745→}
   746→
   747→replayButton.onclick = replayLastRecording;
   748→
   749→function updateReplayButtonState() {
   750→    if (!replayButton) return;
   751→
   752→    if (!storageAvailable) {
   753→        replayButton.disabled = true;
   754→        replayButton.title    = 'Local storage not available';
   755→        return;
   756→    }
   757→    if (isBrainstormRecording || isReplaying || isListening || isBrainstormProcessing) {
   758→        replayButton.disabled = true;
   759→        return;
   760→    }
   761→
   762→    getLatestCompletedSession().then(session => {
   763→        if (!isReplaying) {
   764→            replayButton.disabled = !session;
   765→            replayButton.title    = session ? 'Replay last recording' : 'No recording to replay';
   766→            replayButton.classList.remove('replaying');
   767→        }
   768→    });
   769→}
   770→
   771→/* ===================================================
   772→   INDEXEDDB — stores PCM16 chunks for replay
   773→   =================================================== */
   774→
   775→function createDBStores(event) {
   776→    const d = event.target.result;
   777→    if (!d.objectStoreNames.contains('sessions')) {
   778→        const s = d.createObjectStore('sessions', { keyPath: 'id', autoIncrement: true });
   779→        s.createIndex('status',    'status',    { unique: false });
   780→        s.createIndex('createdAt', 'createdAt', { unique: false });
   781→    }
   782→    if (!d.objectStoreNames.contains('chunks')) {
   783→        const c = d.createObjectStore('chunks', { keyPath: 'id', autoIncrement: true });
   784→        c.createIndex('sessionId', 'sessionId', { unique: false });
   785→        c.createIndex('seq',       'seq',       { unique: false });
   786→    }
   787→}
   788→
   789→async function initIndexedDB() {
   790→    return new Promise((resolve) => {
   791→        const request = indexedDB.open('brainwave-replay', 1);
   792→
   793→        request.onerror = () => {
   794→            console.warn('IndexedDB not available, replay disabled');
   795→            storageAvailable = false;
   796→            resolve(false);
   797→        };
   798→
   799→        request.onsuccess = () => {
   800→            db = request.result;
   801→            if (!db.objectStoreNames.contains('sessions') || !db.objectStoreNames.contains('chunks')) {
   802→                db.close();
   803→                const del = indexedDB.deleteDatabase('brainwave-replay');
   804→                del.onsuccess = () => {
   805→                    const reopen = indexedDB.open('brainwave-replay', 1);
   806→                    reopen.onsuccess       = () => { db = reopen.result; storageAvailable = true; updateReplayButtonState(); resolve(true); };
   807→                    reopen.onerror         = () => { storageAvailable = false; resolve(false); };
   808→                    reopen.onupgradeneeded = createDBStores;
   809→                };
   810→                del.onerror = () => { storageAvailable = false; resolve(false); };
   811→                return;
   812→            }
   813→            storageAvailable = true;
   814→            updateReplayButtonState();
   815→            resolve(true);
   816→        };
   817→
   818→        request.onupgradeneeded = createDBStores;
   819→    });
   820→}
   821→
   822→async function createSession() {
   823→    if (!db) return null;
   824→    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
   825→        const tx    = db.transaction(['sessions'], 'readwrite');
   826→        const store = tx.objectStore('sessions');
   827→        const req   = store.add({ createdAt: new Date(), status: 'recording', sampleRate: 24000, channelCount: 1, durationMs: 0 });
   828→        req.onsuccess = () => {
   829→            currentSessionId  = req.result;
   830→            sessionStartTime  = performance.now();
   831→            chunkSeq          = 0;
   832→            appendChunk(currentSessionId, { seq: 0, deltaMs: 0, kind: 'start', payload: null, byteLength: 0 });
   833→            resolve(currentSessionId);
   834→        };
   835→        req.onerror = () => reject(req.error);
   836→    });
   837→}
   838→
   839→async function appendChunk(sessionId, chunk) {
   840→    if (!db || !sessionId) return;
   841→    return new Promise((resolve) => {
   842→        const tx    = db.transaction(['chunks'], 'readwrite');
   843→        const store = tx.objectStore('chunks');
   844→        const req   = store.add({ sessionId, seq: chunk.seq, deltaMs: chunk.deltaMs, kind: chunk.kind, payload: chunk.payload, byteLength: chunk.byteLength });
   845→        req.onsuccess = () => resolve();
   846→        req.onerror   = () => resolve(); // don't fail recording on storage error
   847→    });
   848→}
   849→
   850→async function completeSession(sessionId, durationMs) {
   851→    if (!db || !sessionId) return;
   852→    return new Promise((resolve) => {
   853→        const tx            = db.transaction(['sessions', 'chunks'], 'readwrite');
   854→        const sessionsStore = tx.objectStore('sessions');
   855→        const chunksStore   = tx.objectStore('chunks');
   856→        const req           = sessionsStore.get(sessionId);
   857→        req.onsuccess = () => {
   858→            const sess = req.result;
   859→            sess.status    = 'completed';
   860→            sess.durationMs = durationMs;
   861→            sessionsStore.put(sess);
   862→            chunksStore.add({ sessionId, seq: chunkSeq++, deltaMs: durationMs, kind: 'stop', payload: null, byteLength: 0 });
   863→            enforceQuota({ maxSessions: 5 });
   864→            resolve();
   865→        };
   866→        req.onerror = () => resolve();
   867→    });
   868→}
   869→
   870→async function enforceQuota({ maxSessions }) {
   871→    if (!db) return;
   872→    const tx            = db.transaction(['sessions', 'chunks'], 'readwrite');
   873→    const sessionsStore = tx.objectStore('sessions');
   874→    const sessions      = [];
   875→    sessionsStore.index('createdAt').openCursor().onsuccess = (event) => {
   876→        const cursor = event.target.result;
   877→        if (cursor) { sessions.push(cursor.value); cursor.continue(); }
   878→        else {
   879→            sessions.sort((a, b) => a.createdAt - b.createdAt);
   880→            while (sessions.length > maxSessions) deleteSession(sessions.shift().id);
   881→        }
   882→    };
   883→}
   884→
   885→async function deleteSession(sessionId) {
   886→    if (!db) return;
   887→    const tx            = db.transaction(['sessions', 'chunks'], 'readwrite');
   888→    const sessionsStore = tx.objectStore('sessions');
   889→    const chunksStore   = tx.objectStore('chunks');
   890→    chunksStore.index('sessionId').openKeyCursor(IDBKeyRange.only(sessionId)).onsuccess = (event) => {
   891→        const cursor = event.target.result;
   892→        if (cursor) { chunksStore.delete(cursor.primaryKey); cursor.continue(); }
   893→    };
   894→    sessionsStore.delete(sessionId);
   895→}
   896→
   897→async function getLatestCompletedSession() {
   898→    if (!db) return null;
   899→    return new Promise((resolve) => {
   900→        const tx    = db.transaction(['sessions'], 'readonly');
   901→        const req   = tx.objectStore('sessions').index('status').getAll('completed');
   902→        req.onsuccess = () => {
   903→            const sessions = req.result;
   904→            if (!sessions.length) { resolve(null); return; }
   905→            sessions.sort((a, b) => b.createdAt - a.createdAt);
   906→            resolve(sessions[0]);
   907→        };
   908→        req.onerror = () => resolve(null);
   909→    });
   910→}
   911→
   912→async function getSessionChunks(sessionId) {
   913→    if (!db || !sessionId) return [];
   914→    return new Promise((resolve) => {
   915→        const tx  = db.transaction(['chunks'], 'readonly');
   916→        const req = tx.objectStore('chunks').index('sessionId').getAll(sessionId);
   917→        req.onsuccess = () => {
   918→            const chunks = req.result;
   919→            chunks.sort((a, b) => a.seq - b.seq);
   920→            resolve(chunks);
   921→        };
   922→        req.onerror = () => resolve([]);
   923→    });
   924→}
   925→
   926→/* ===== KEYBOARD SHORTCUT ===== */
   927→document.addEventListener('keydown', (event) => {
   928→    if (event.code === 'Space') {
   929→        const el = document.activeElement;
   930→        if (!el.tagName.match(/INPUT|TEXTAREA|SELECT/) && !el.isContentEditable) {
   931→            event.preventDefault();
   932→            if (isListening) {
   933→                stopQuickMode();
   934→            } else if (isBrainstormRecording) {
   935→                stopBrainstormRecording();
   936→            } else if (!isBrainstormProcessing && !isReplaying) {
   937→                startQuickMode();
   938→            }
   939→        }
   940→    }
   941→});
   942→
   943→/* ===== INIT ===== */
   944→document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', async () => {
   945→    await initIndexedDB();
   946→
   947→    if (!SpeechRecognition) {
   948→        notSupported.hidden = false;
   949→        quickBtn.disabled   = true;
   950→        quickBtn.title      = 'Speech recognition not supported in this browser';
   951→    } else {
   952→        initRecognition();
   953→    }
   954→
   955→    initializeWebSocket();
   956→});

488\u2192\n   489\u2192/* ===== Audio processing ===== */\n   490\u2192function createAudioProcessor() {\n   491\u2192    processor = audioContext.createScriptProcessor(4096, 1, 1);\n   492\u2192        });\n   519\u2192                }\n   520\u2192            }\n   521\u2192        }\n   522\u2192    };\n   523\u2192    return processor;\n   524\u2192}\n   525\u2192\n   526\u2192async   670\u2192\n   671\u2192/* ===================================================\n   672\u2192   REPLAY \u2014 sends stored IndexedDB audio through WS\n   673\u2192 715\u2192        }\n   716\u2192\n   717\u2192        ws.send(JSON.stringify({ type: 'stop_recording' }));\n   718\u2192\n   719\u2192        isBrainstormProcessing    = true;\n   720\u2192   "new_string": "/* ===== BRAINSTORM POST-PROCESSING ===== */\n\nfunction getBackendBaseUrl() {\n    const backendUrl = localStorage.getItem('brainwaveBackendUrl') || '';\n    if (backendUrl) {\n        try {\n            const url = new URL(backendUrl);\n            return `${url.protocol}//${url.host}`;\n        } catch (_) { /* fall through to default */ }\n    }\n    return `${window.location.protocol}//${window.location.host}`;\n}\n\nlet _postprocessedContent = '';\n\nasync function runPostProcess(endpoint, label, activeBtn) {\n    const text = transcriptText.textContent.trim();\n    if (!text) return;\n\n    // Reset result area\n    _postprocessedContent = '';\n    postprocessText.textContent = '';\n    postprocessLabel.textContent = label;\n    postprocessResultActions.hidden = true;\n\n    // Disable both buttons; show loading on the active one\n    readabilityBtn.disabled = true;\n    inspireBtn.disabled = true;\n    const origLabel = activeBtn.textContent;\n    activeBtn.textContent = 'Processing\u2026';\n\n    // Show the result area (empty initially so user sees it appeared)\n    postprocessResult.hidden = false;\n\n    try {\n        const response = await fetch(`${getBackendBaseUrl()}${endpoint}`, {\n            method:  'POST',\n            headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n            body:    JSON.stringify({ text }),\n        });\n\n        if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`HTTP ${response.status}`);\n\n        const reader  = response.body.getReader();\n        const decoder = new TextDecoder();\n\n        while (true) {\n            const { done, value } = await reader.read();\n            if (done) break;\n            _postprocessedContent += decoder.decode(value, { stream: true });\n            postprocessText.textContent = _postprocessedContent;\n        }\n\n        // Streaming complete \u2014 show Send button\n        postprocessResultActions.hidden = false;\n\n    } catch (err) {\n        console.error('Post-processing error:', err);\n        postprocessText.textContent = 'Error: could not process. Check connection and try again.';\n    } finally {\n        activeBtn.textContent = origLabel;\n        readabilityBtn.disabled = false;\n        inspireBtn.disabled = false;\n    }\n}\n\nreadabilityBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {\n    runPostProcess('/api/v1/readability', 'Readability', readabilityBtn);\n});\n\ninspireBtn.addEventListener('click', () => {\n    runPostProcess('/api/v1/correctness', 'Inspire', inspireBtn);\n});\n\npostprocessSendBtn.addEventListener('click', async () => {\n    const text = _postprocessedContent.trim();\n    if (!text) return;\n    hideTranscriptBar();\n    await sendMessage(text, 'brainstorm');\n});\n\n/* ===== SETTINGS MODAL ===== */"
